[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   | If you ever happen to want to link against installed libraries
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   | in a given directory, LIBDIR, you must either use libtool, and
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   | specify the full pathname of the library, or use the `-LLIBDIR'
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   | flag during linking and do at least one of the following:
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   |    - add LIBDIR to the `LD_LIBRARY_PATH' environment variable
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   |      during execution
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   |    - add LIBDIR to the `LD_RUN_PATH' environment variable
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   |      during linking
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   |    - use the `-Wl,-rpath -Wl,LIBDIR' linker flag
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   |    - have your system administrator add LIBDIR to `/etc/ld.so.conf'
[Flatpak/Flatpak Build Steps/Flatpak Build]   |
